add_namespace = WORLD
add_namespace = novel #for althist novels

# Hitler is dead - natural
news_event = {
	id = WORLD.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event WORLD.1"}

	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = hitler_dead
		GER = {
			news_event = {
				id = reich.23
			}
		}
		USA = {
			news_event = {
				id = USA.10
			}
		}
		BRG = {
			news_event = {
				id = BRG.10
			}
		}
		JAP = {
			news_event = {
				id = JAP.10
			}
		}
		ENG = {
			news_event = {
				id = ENG.10
			}
		}
		FFR = {
			news_event = {
				id = FREEDOM.10
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = WORLD.1.a
	}
}

news_event = { # The German Civil War
	id = WORLD.5
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event WORLD.5"}
	title = WORLD.5.t
	desc = WORLD.5.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_german_civil_war

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = WORLD.5.a
		if = {
			limit = { is_ai = no }
			set_country_flag = big_event_german_civil_war
			hidden_effect = { BRG = { TNO_BRG_domestic_tree_swap = yes } }
		}
	}
}

# Assassin strikes the fuhrer
news_event = {
	id = WORLD.9
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event WORLD.9"}

	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	#trigger = {
		#	date > 1962.1.20
		#	NOT = { has_global_flag = assassin_attacks_hitler }
		#}

	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = assassin_attacks_hitler
		GER = {
			news_event = {
				id = reich.5
			}
		}
		USA = {
			news_event = {
				id = USA.12
			}
		}
		#		BRG = {
			#			news_event = {
				#				id = BRG.10
				#			}
			#		}
		#		JAP = {
			#			news_event = {
				#				id = JAP.10
				#			}
			#		}
		#		ENG = {
			#			news_event = {
				#				id = ENG.10
				#			}
			#		}
		#		FFR = {
			#			news_event = {
				#				id = FREEDOM.10
				#			}
			#		}
		every_country = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							tag = GER tag = USA tag = JAP tag = ENG tag = FFR
						}
					}
				}
				news_event = {
					id = WORLD.34
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = WORLD.1.a
	}
}

	id = WORLD.18
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event WORLD.18"}

	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	immediate = {
		clr_global_flag = hawaiian_missile_crisis

				id = USA.70
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							tag = USA
						}
					}
				}
				news_event = {
					id = WORLD.70
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = WORLD.18.a

news_event = { #GCW contenders all at war - Caused by an on_action after peace confrences, trigger there to make sure doesn't happen after GCW is over or other silly situations
	id = WORLD.25
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event WORLD.25"}

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = anti_heydrich_pact }
		has_global_flag = german_civil_war
		NOT = { has_global_flag = german_civil_war_end }
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				OR = {
					NOT = { country_exists = SGR}
					has_war_with = SGR
					tag = SGR
				}
				OR = {
					NOT = { country_exists = HGR}
					has_war_with = HGR
					tag = HGR
				}
				OR = {
					NOT = { country_exists = BGR}
					has_war_with = BGR
					tag = BGR
				}
				OR = {
					NOT = { country_exists = GGR}
					has_war_with = GGR
					tag = GGR
				}
				OR = {
					NOT = { country_exists = DSR}
					has_war_with = DSR
					tag = DSR
				}
				OR = {
					NOT = { country_exists = RNW}
					has_war_with = RNW
					tag = RNW
				}
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = SGR }
				country_exists = SGR
				NOT = { has_war_with = SGR }
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = SGR
				type = civil_war
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = GGR }
				country_exists = GGR
				NOT = { has_war_with = GGR }
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = GGR
				type = civil_war
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = BGR }
				country_exists = BGR
				NOT = { has_war_with = BGR }
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = BGR
				type = civil_war
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = HGR }
				country_exists = HGR
				NOT = { has_war_with = HGR }
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = HGR
				type = civil_war
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = DSR }
				country_exists = DSR
				NOT = { has_war_with = DSR }
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = DSR
				type = civil_war
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = RNW }
				country_exists = RNW
				NOT = { has_war_with = RNW }
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = RNW
				type = civil_war
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = WORLD.25.a
	}
}

##Anti-Heydrich Coalition Chain
news_event = {
	id = WORLD.26
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event WORLD.26"}
	title = WORLD.26.t
	desc = WORLD.26.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_nazi_moon

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = HGR
		OR = { #balancing with prussia, to avoid where either keeping prussia to avoid bad balance by leaving/keeping prussia fucks up the number
			AND = {
				num_of_controlled_states > 7
				NOT = { 188 = { is_owned_by = HGR } }
				NOT = { 85 = { is_owned_by = HGR } }
				NOT = { 5 = { is_owned_by = HGR } }
				NOT = { 98 = { is_owned_by = HGR } }
				NOT = { 97 = { is_owned_by = HGR } }
			}
			AND = {
				num_of_controlled_states > 8
				count_triggers = {
					amount = 4
					NOT = { 188 = { is_owned_by = HGR } }
					NOT = { 85 = { is_owned_by = HGR } }
					NOT = { 5 = { is_owned_by = HGR } }
					NOT = { 98 = { is_owned_by = HGR } }
					NOT = { 97 = { is_owned_by = HGR } }
				}
			}
			# redundant?
			#AND = {
				#num_of_controlled_states > 8
				#count_triggers = {
					#amount = 3
					#NOT = { 188 = { is_owned_by = HGR }}
					#NOT = { 85 = { is_owned_by = HGR }}
					#NOT = { 5 = { is_owned_by = HGR }}
					#NOT = { 98 = { is_owned_by = HGR }}
					#NOT = { 97 = { is_owned_by = HGR }}
				#}
			#}
			AND = {
				num_of_controlled_states > 9
				count_triggers = {
					amount = 3
					NOT = { 188 = { is_owned_by = HGR } }
					NOT = { 85 = { is_owned_by = HGR } }
					NOT = { 5 = { is_owned_by = HGR } }
					NOT = { 98 = { is_owned_by = HGR } }
					NOT = { 97 = { is_owned_by = HGR } }
				}
			}
			AND = {
				num_of_controlled_states > 10
				count_triggers = {
					amount = 2
					NOT = { 188 = { is_owned_by = HGR } }
					NOT = { 85 = { is_owned_by = HGR } }
					NOT = { 5 = { is_owned_by = HGR } }
					NOT = { 98 = { is_owned_by = HGR } }
					NOT = { 97 = { is_owned_by = HGR } }
				}
			}
			AND = {
				num_of_controlled_states > 11
				count_triggers = {
					amount = 1
					NOT = { 188 = { is_owned_by = HGR } }
					NOT = { 85 = { is_owned_by = HGR } }
					NOT = { 5 = { is_owned_by = HGR } }
					NOT = { 98 = { is_owned_by = HGR } }
					NOT = { 97 = { is_owned_by = HGR } }
				}
			}
			AND = {
				num_of_controlled_states > 12
				188 = { is_owned_by = HGR }
				85 = { is_owned_by = HGR }
				5 = { is_owned_by = HGR }
				98 = { is_owned_by = HGR }
				97 = { is_owned_by = HGR }
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				count_triggers = { #if only one left, ignore
					amount > 1
					country_exists = BGR
					country_exists = SGR
					country_exists = GGR
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = SGR
				}
				SGR = {
					country_event = {
						id = speer.16 #start chain
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { country_exists = SGR }
					country_exists = BGR
				}
				BGR = {
					country_event = {
						id = bormann.9 #start chain
					}
					} #if both are dead then there is only Goering left, so the chain has no reason to start
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = WORLD.26.a
	}
}

# Anti-Heydrich Pact
news_event = {
	id = WORLD.28
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event WORLD.28"}
	title = WORLD.28.t
	desc = WORLD.28.desc
	picture = GFX_news_event_nuremberg_ruins

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = WORLD.28.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				original_tag = BGR
				original_tag = GGR
				original_tag = SGR
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = WORLD.28.b
		trigger = {
			original_tag = HGR
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = WORLD.28.c
		trigger = {
			original_tag = BRG
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = WORLD.28.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					original_tag = BGR
					original_tag = GGR
					original_tag = SGR
					original_tag = HGR
					original_tag = BRG
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

news_event = {
	id = WORLD.29
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event WORLD.29"}
	title = WORLD.29.t
	desc = WORLD.29.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_nazi_moon

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	immediate = {
		if = { #give everyone their occupied land
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = BGR }
			}
			BGR = {
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }
					ROOT = {
						set_state_owner = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = GGR }
			}
			GGR = {
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }
					ROOT = {
						set_state_owner = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = SGR }
			}
			SGR = {
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }
					ROOT = {
						set_state_owner = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = HGR } #incase of weird scenarios like migration
			}
			HGR = {
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }
					ROOT = {
						set_state_owner = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = BGR
			}
			news_event = {
				id = WORLD.30
				days = 1
			}
			create_faction = anti_heydrich_pact_faction
			if = { #whitepeacing
				limit = {
					BGR = {
						has_country_flag = anti_heydrich_pact
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						GGR = {
							has_country_flag = anti_heydrich_pact
						}
					}
					GGR = {
						white_peace = BGR
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = GGR
			}
			BGR = {
				news_event = {
					id = WORLD.29
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = WORLD.29.a
	}
}

	id = WORLD.30

	desc = WORLD.30.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_nazi_moon

			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = WORLD.30.a
	}
}

news_event = {
	id = WORLD.32
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event WORLD.32"}
	title = WORLD.32.t
	desc = WORLD.32.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_nazi_moon

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			country_exists = HGR
			has_global_flag = german_civil_war_end
		}
		has_country_flag = anti_heydrich_pact
	}
	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = anti_heydrich_pact
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
				tag = SGR
			}
			SGR = {
				dismantle_faction  = yes
				if = {
					limit = {
						count_triggers = { #if only one left, ignore
							amount > 1
							country_exists = BGR
							country_exists = SGR
							country_exists = GGR
						}
					}
					news_event = {
						id = WORLD.33
						days = 1
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
				tag = BGR
			}
			BGR = {
				dismantle_faction  = yes
				if = {
					limit = {
						count_triggers = { #if only one left, ignore
							amount > 1
							country_exists = BGR
							country_exists = SGR
							country_exists = GGR
						}
					}
					news_event = {
						id = WORLD.33
						days = 1
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
				tag = GGR
			}
			GGR = {
				dismantle_faction  = yes
				if = {
					limit = {
						count_triggers = { #if only one left, ignore
							amount > 1
							country_exists = BGR
							country_exists = SGR
							country_exists = GGR
						}
					}
					news_event = {
						id = WORLD.33
						days = 1
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = WORLD.32.a
	}
}

news_event = {
	id = WORLD.33
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event WORLD.33"}
	title = WORLD.33.t
	desc = WORLD.33.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_nazi_moon

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = BGR
			}
			BGR = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						country_exists = GGR
					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = GGR
						type = civil_war
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						country_exists = SGR
					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = SGR
						type = civil_war
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = GGR
				country_exists = SGR
			}
			GGR = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = SGR
					type = civil_war
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = WORLD.33.a
	}
}

# Yemeni Civil War
news_event = {
	id = WORLD.50
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event WORLD.50"}
	title = WORLD.50.t
	desc = WORLD.50.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_yemen_war
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = arab_war_ongoing
	}

	immediate = {
		ITA = {
			news_event = {
				id = WORLD.51
			}
		}
		YEM = {
			news_event = {
				id = YEM.51
			}
		}
		NYM = {
			news_event = {
				id = WORLD.51
			}
		}
		OMA = {
			news_event = {
				id = OMA.50
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							tag = ITA tag = YEM tag = NYM tag = OMA
						}
					}
				}
				news_event = {
					id = WORLD.51
				}
			}
		}
	}

	

	option = {
		name = WORLD.50.a
	}

}

	id = WORLD.420 #socialists win 79

	title = WORLD.420.t
	desc = WORLD.420.desc
	picture = GFX_news_event_india_narain_1979

	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		RAJ = {
			has_country_flag = RAJ_soc_4
		}
	}

	option = { #India
		name = WORLD.420.a
		trigger = {
			original_tag = RAJ
		}
	}
	option = { #Everyone Else
		name = WORLD.420.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				original_tag = RAJ
				has_government = communist
				has_government = socialist
				RAJ = {
					has_country_flag = RAJ_soc_3
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #other lib/authsoc countries
		name = WORLD.400.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				original_tag = RAJ
			}
			OR = {
				has_government = communist
				has_government = socialist
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #more of the same
		name = WORLD.402.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				original_tag = RAJ

					has_government = communist
					has_government = socialist
				}
			}
			RAJ = {
				has_country_flag = RAJ_soc_3
			}
		}
	}

	title = WORLD.669.t
	desc = WORLD.669.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_terrorist_attack_italy

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event WORLD.669" }

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = WORLD.669.a
	}
}

#All world events 700-899 claimed by AMERICA






#US President World Events
#RD-D is 1, RD-R 2, NPP-C 3, NPP-FR 4, NPP-R 5, NPP-L 6
#70x is 1964
news_event = { #Wallace F. Bennett
	id = WORLD.701
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event WORLD.701"}
	title = WORLD.701.t
	desc = WORLD.701.desc
	picture = GFX_news_event_usa_wallace_bennett

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = WORLD.701.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = GER
				is_in_faction_with = GER
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = WORLD.701.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = JAP
				is_in_faction_with = JAP
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = WORLD.701.c
		trigger = {
			is_in_faction_with = USA
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = WORLD.701.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					tag = GER
					tag = JAP
					is_in_faction_with = USA
					is_in_faction_with = GER
					is_in_faction_with = JAP
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

news_event = { #Algerian war
	id = WORLD.915
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event WORLD.915"}
	title = WORLD.915.t
	desc = WORLD.915.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_algeria_war

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = WORLD.915.a

		trigger =  {
			original_tag = ITA
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = WORLD.915.b

		trigger =  {
			original_tag = IBR
		}

		clr_country_flag = IBR_decisions_post_trium
		set_country_flag = IBR_decisions_foreign
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Francisco Franco"
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {IBR_caudillo_correct_var = 1}
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = IBRIberiaStability
			value = -1
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = IBR_sub_stability_small_tt

		custom_effect_tooltip = IBR_pp_foreign_get_tt
		
		hidden_effect = { 
			country_event = { 
				id = IBR.31051
				days = 10
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = WORLD.915.c

		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					original_tag = ITA
					original_tag = IBR
				}
			}
		}
	}

}

		}
	}
}

news_event = { #The Magadan Conference
	id = WORLD.2019
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event WORLD.2019"}
	title = WORLD.2019.t
	desc = WORLD.2019.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_komi_socdems
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = WORLD.2019.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_government = socialist
				has_government = communist
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = WORLD.2019.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_government = socialist
					has_government = communist
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

news_event = { #ENG - Anglo-Scottish War English Victory
	id = WORLD.50009
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event WORLD.50009" }
	title = WORLD.50009.t
	desc = WORLD.50009.desc
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_news_event_ENG_SCO_Unification_Peaceful

	option = { #england
		name = WORLD.50009.a
		trigger = {
			tag = ENG
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_ai = no }
			if = {
				limit = { ENG = { has_country_flag = NDL_victorious } }
				set_country_flag = big_event_british_reunification_jellicoe
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { ENG = { has_country_flag = SLP_victorious } }
				set_country_flag = big_event_british_reunification_wilson
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { ENG = { has_country_flag = ENG_Thatcher_victorious } }
				set_country_flag = big_event_british_reunification_thatcher
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { ENG = { has_country_flag = ENG_mac_shadowmaster } }
				set_country_flag = big_event_british_reunification_mac
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { ENG = { has_country_flag = ENG_mac_liberal } }
				set_country_flag = big_event_british_reunification_maudling
			}		
		}
	}

	option = { #world
		name = WORLD.50009.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = ENG
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_ai = no }
			if = {
				limit = { ENG = { has_country_flag = NDL_victorious } }
				set_country_flag = big_event_british_reunification_jellicoe
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { ENG = { has_country_flag = SLP_victorious } }
				set_country_flag = big_event_british_reunification_wilson
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { ENG = { has_country_flag = ENG_Thatcher_victorious } }
				set_country_flag = big_event_british_reunification_thatcher
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { ENG = { has_country_flag = ENG_mac_shadowmaster } }
				set_country_flag = big_event_british_reunification_mac
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { ENG = { has_country_flag = ENG_mac_liberal } }
				set_country_flag = big_event_british_reunification_maudling
			}		
		}
	}
}

news_event = { #Goering Germany declares war on Burgundy for Fall Schwarz
	id = WORLD.14999
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event WORLD.14999" }
	title = WORLD.14999.t
	desc = WORLD.14999.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_news_event_madagaskar_civil_war


	option = { #We will crush the traitors
		name = WORLD.14999.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = GER
				is_in_faction_with = GER
			}
		}
        if = {
            limit = {
                is_ai = no
            }
            set_country_flag = big_event_fall_schwarz
        }
	}


	option = { #THe decadent fools will face their doom
		name = WORLD.14999.b
		trigger = {
			tag = BRG
		}
        if = {
            limit = {
                is_ai = no
            }
            set_country_flag = big_event_fall_schwarz
        }
	}

	option = { #The final battle is come
		name = WORLD.14999.c
		trigger = {
			has_government = burgundian_system
			NOT = {
				tag = BRG
			}
		}
        if = {
            limit = {
                is_ai = no
            }
            set_country_flag = big_event_fall_schwarz
        }
	}

	option = {	#Oh my god!
		name = WORLD.14999.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					tag = BRG
					tag = GER
					is_in_faction_with = GER
				}
			}
			OR = {
				has_government = communist
				has_government = ultranational_socialism
				has_government = national_socialism
				has_government = fascism
				has_government = social_conservative
				has_government = social_democrat
				has_government = social_liberal
				has_government = socialist
			}
		}
        if = {
            limit = {
                is_ai = no
            }
            set_country_flag = big_event_fall_schwarz
        }
	}
}
